  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d257647e-501d-4345-b76b-7131cf517827'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <i>Wedding Day</i>
</b><br /><br />Pretty, flighty Daisy Devreaux can either go to jail or marry the mystery man her father has chosen for her. Arranged marriages don't happen in the modern world, so how did the irrepressible Daisy find herself in this fix?<br /><br />Alex Markov, as humorless as he is deadly handsome, has no intention of playing the loving bridegroom to a spoiled little feather-head with champagne tastes. He drags Daisy from her uptown life to a broken down traveling circus and sets out to tame her to his ways.<br /><br />But this man without a soul has met his match in a woman who's nothing but heart. Before long, passion will send them flying sky high without a safety net... risking it all in search of a love that will last forever.</span>

<a href="/questions/1047856-i-read-this-book-last-year-and-i">I read this book last year and I absolutely loved it! Does anyone know if there are more books like this one??? It does not have to be about arranged marriages, but I need some alpha-male and a likeable heroine. 
I already read the unwanted wife, which was an okay read, but nothing close to Kiss an angel.</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=at-home-book-shelf">at-home-book-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=jerks">jerks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4482512-jennifer?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146405704" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14443793148214492281"><b>5,000 CIRCUS STARS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>You HAVE to read this book!!! Please. I’m begging you, fellow readers.</b><br/><br/><img alt='image' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380345295ra/699977.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is not your typical story. This is not your typical book. <b>This is a story that you have never read….trust me.</b> It is anything BUT typical. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699978.jpg' alt='Love the idea of a black and white photo of vintage circus tents' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story begins with an arranged marriage. No, it’s not set in the medieval times. It’s a modern arranged marriage. Say what?! I know. It seems off-putting at first. But we quickly get to know Alex and Daisy, and the reason for the arranged marriage takes an app</span>
  <span id="freeText14443793148214492281" style="display:none"><b>5,000 CIRCUS STARS!!!!!!</b><br><br><b>You HAVE to read this book!!! Please. I’m begging you, fellow readers.</b><br><br><img alt="image" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380345295ra/699977.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is not your typical story. This is not your typical book. <b>This is a story that you have never read….trust me.</b> It is anything BUT typical. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699978.jpg" alt="Love the idea of a black and white photo of vintage circus tents" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins with an arranged marriage. No, it’s not set in the medieval times. It’s a modern arranged marriage. Say what?! I know. It seems off-putting at first. But we quickly get to know Alex and Daisy, and the reason for the arranged marriage takes an approved back seat for a while. <br><br>This story is set <b>at the circus.</b> Yes, I said the circus. Weird?? Absolutely not. Mainly because <b>SEP is a genius.</b> Alex is a trained expert with bull <b>whips.</b> Yep, it’s gets dirty real fast, ladies. No, he doesn’t actually whip her (for those of you who are afraid of reads that are too dark, although I wouldn’t mind a little whipping, heeheehee), but the promise of whipping is there. The sexual chemistry and witty dialogue are <b>off the charts. </b><br><br><b>
  <i>We can do this easy, or we can do it rough. Either way, I'm going to win. You decide how it'll be.</i>
</b><br><br><b>My Alex:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699979._SY540_.jpg" alt="Kostas Martakis" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699980.jpg" alt="...and any man may find himself on the chain, or drawn agonisingly on the post, screaming under the fire of her lash! And yet...a man may adore her so utterly..." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alex. Alex. Alex. I would die for him. What a fantastic character. He was abused by the whip when he was a boy. He believes he is literally incapable of love. He is mysterious because he doesn’t reveal much about himself to Daisy. He purposefully tries to push her away because he doesn’t want her to fall in love with him. He doesn’t even want her to get comfortable, so he puts her through hell, expecting her to give up. <b>I love LOVE/HATE relationships! They make the best sex!!!!</b><br><br><b>My Daisy:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699981.jpg" alt="violet" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>But I don't love you, Daisy, and you can't begin to know how sorry I am about that because if I could choose anyone in this world to love, it'd be you.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699982._SY540_.jpg" alt="so precious" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though Alex is trying to make Daisy give up, she won’t. She is stubborn and strong. <b>Daisy is all heart.</b> She might have a spoiled side, but when she loves, she loves with everything she’s got. She forms an attachment to the circus animals, and to say that the attachment is endearing would be an understatement. The way SEP writes these animals <b>captivated me.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Like the circus animals, she was held captive against her will, and, like them, her keeper had all the power.</i>
</b><br><br><img alt="" width="500" height="269" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699983.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>She was in a warm elephant cave. She pressed her cheek to his scratchy, gunnysack body just between his legs and heard the strong thud of his sweet, mischievous heart. She knew she should move, but even though she was resting beneath a ton of baby elephant, she had never felt safer. As she sat there, she thought of Alex and wished he were small enough to fit where she was, right beneath Tater's heart.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699984.jpg" alt="For Angela" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SEP has a talent for writing a complete, no-page-unturned, no-character-left-behind story. She always includes a full story of the B characters, and I always love it. She gives everyone an HEA. Here are a couple of the B characters that I loved.<br><br>Sheba is the circus owner. She is hard-headed, stubborn, prideful….a bitch. She cares for the circus and the people in the circus with everything she’s got…except for Daisy, which makes it interesting. I can’t help but love her.<br><br><b>My Sheba:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699985._SY540_.jpg" alt="Sheba - kiss an angel" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Heather is a teenage girl caught in the middle of growing up. She is trying to earn the love of her father by trying her best to be a good circus performer. She plays a key role in the story, and forms an attachment to Daisy.<br><br><b>My Heather:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345295i/699986._SY540_.jpg" alt="Heather - Kiss and Angel" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Note to Susan: <br><br>Dear Susan,</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380345295ra/699987.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Cheers. Cheers to this book. Cheers this story. Cheers these characters. Cheers to YOU.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380345295ra/699988.gif" alt="" width="500px" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is officially in my top 3 favorites SEP books. <br><br><b>This is a must-read. This is a re-read. Read it.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14443793148214492281" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_126508083" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/126508083" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/126508083?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780061794797" href="/book/show/9482513-kiss-an-angel">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=cont-romance">cont-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer126508083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4166417902487770543">Do you know that feeling when you have just finished a book you adored but you just can't figure out how to express that on your review? Well that's exactly what happened to me but I'll do my best to try to explain it to you all.<br/><br/>This was my favorite book from this author, I even liked it more than the Chicago stars series and I already had adored that one, I gave 5 stars to most of the books in it. But it was so different this time. I couldn't put the book down, that's how FREAKING amazing it wa</span>
  <span id="freeText4166417902487770543" style="display:none">Do you know that feeling when you have just finished a book you adored but you just can't figure out how to express that on your review? Well that's exactly what happened to me but I'll do my best to try to explain it to you all.<br /><br />This was my favorite book from this author, I even liked it more than the Chicago stars series and I already had adored that one, I gave 5 stars to most of the books in it. But it was so different this time. I couldn't put the book down, that's how FREAKING amazing it was for me. I loved this book so much. I even cried like a baby with it. My heart felt like it would break into a million pieces more than once, while some other times I felt like I would go crazy for feeling so happy about fictional characters, lol, but seriously I totally connected with them.<br /><br />In this book we get to meet Alex, our sexy Russian hero. He was so lost and suffering so much through life without even realizing it. He had been abused by his uncle as a child (by being knocked down and brutalized) and was sure he just wasn't able to love anyone or anything. It's not like he had not tried, he had, but he thought he could never get to love someone, that he was broken inside. It was so heartbreaking to see how he could not accept so many great things that started to happen to him but at the same time it was so emotional to see him accepting them at the end. He was the best part of the book IMHO. The rest of the characters were amazing as well. So be ready for a great ride with this book because you'll experience tons of emotions in just a couple of hundred of pages,lol.<br /><br />I just can't understand how this author keeps surprising me this way. I'm so obsessed with her right now! Its like every new book I read from her is even better than the last one. I never thought I would like Contemporary romance but I know I do now. Can't wait to read another book from this author, I just can't get enough.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4166417902487770543" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15586682-lady-gabriella-of-awesomeness-slow?shelf=2013-favourites">2013-favourites</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15586682-lady-gabriella-of-awesomeness-slow?shelf=angst">angst</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15586682-lady-gabriella-of-awesomeness-slow?shelf=read-n-reviewed">read-n-reviewed</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer527058970" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4595387993462702462"><b>
  <i>OMG...I cant even...This love story just blew me away..... </i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg' width='400' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>"I don't love you anymore,Alex."<br/>"It's alright sweetheart.I love you enough for the both of us."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453727146ra/17863192.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg' width='400' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>KISS AN ANGEL </b> is a beautiful love story that revolves around two broken & loney souls,both vulnerable and lost in their own ways...<br/><br/>Honestly speaking,this book surprised me in more ways than one.I mean with its chic-lite cover,and the book's subtle summary.I had no clue,how emotional this book would really turn out to be.<br/><br/>The characters </span>
  <span id="freeText4595387993462702462" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>OMG...I cant even...This love story just blew me away..... </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"I don't love you anymore,Alex."<br>"It's alright sweetheart.I love you enough for the both of us."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453727146ra/17863192.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>KISS AN ANGEL </b> is a beautiful love story that revolves around two broken &amp; loney souls,both vulnerable and lost in their own ways...<br><br>Honestly speaking,this book surprised me in more ways than one.I mean with its chic-lite cover,and the book's subtle summary.I had no clue,how emotional this book would really turn out to be.<br><br>The characters in the book seemed so individually strong and memorable in their own right.I couldn't help but admire the way Ms.Phillips built a plot around such diverse characters instead of concentrating on just the two main leads.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408236i/798531.jpg" width="500" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I found daisy and (the tiger) sinjun's relationship to be so the most touching.The way she relates to the beast calming &amp; loving him while making way for her own self-discovery was just so complexly written.I adored it ! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>Pride had kept her running when love had betrayed her.</b>
</i><br><br><img alt="Tumblr_mh3arsffox1s1qvcpo1_500_large" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408236i/798532._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440882598i/16036607.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes..It's true.THIS BOOK MADE ME CRY..LIKE A LOT... especially towards the end.The sad misunderstandings that Alex and Daisy go through...seriously,I was a mess.<br><br><b>
  <u>RECOMMENDATION </u>
</b>:This book has permanently earned a place on my <i>favorites shelf</i>. I would highly recommended this book to anybody wanting a good emotional read if they have a LOT of spare time that day because trust me.You would want to finish this in one solid reading.<br><br>Seriously a great book, completely deserves to be read, at least once. <br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2429018441?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2429018441" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12915887918900284650"><b>4.25 Stars <i>(Originally Read - 6/22/2018)</i></b><br/><br/><b>4.25 Stars <i>(Re-Read -1/20/2020)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>Wow! This was so much better than I thought it'd be! I know I might be giving too much away here -- but I think keeping the circus aspect of this book a secret is a poor choice! I might've picked this up sooner if I had known what all we experienced with that! It's an older book, but it really didn't feel all that dated tbh -- maybe the clothing descriptions, but that's about it. I came across this again when</span>
  <span id="freeText12915887918900284650" style="display:none"><b>4.25 Stars <i>(Originally Read - 6/22/2018)</i></b><br /><br /><b>4.25 Stars <i>(Re-Read -1/20/2020)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>Wow! This was so much better than I thought it'd be! I know I might be giving too much away here -- but I think keeping the circus aspect of this book a secret is a poor choice! I might've picked this up sooner if I had known what all we experienced with that! It's an older book, but it really didn't feel all that dated tbh -- maybe the clothing descriptions, but that's about it. I came across this again when I asked GR friends and followers what their favorite re-read books are, and I can totally understand where this would come in! I think it's going on my favorites shelf and will probably be a re-read again farther down the line. Why not 5 Stars then, you ask? The sexual chemistry felt lacking. It wasn't fade-to-black or anything, but I felt like the scenes could've been better. I'm also a greedy, greedy girl and I like my epilogues! This one was alright. I didn't hate it or anything, but I definitely think it could've been a lot better! So with the epilogue/ending (.5 points) and the sexual chemistry (.25 points), I'm going with a 4.25 star rating.<br /><br /><b>*Re-Read Update:</b> I don't have much to add to my original review. I enjoyed this as a re-read but was still let down my the sexual chemistry and the ending. Otherwise, I still found it a great read! It'll probably be one that I re-read again down the line too, as it just is that fun 🤗<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Daisy and Alex's story. Daisy finds herself forced to marry a man of her father's choosing or face jail time. Alex is a mysterious older man that is up for the job for at least the 6 months she is required to stay married before getting her inheritance. Daisy is shocked when Alex swoops her up to get on a plane that takes her to Florida where they join the traveling circus he works for. There is a lot of big adjustments Daisy has to make to fit in with this new lifestyle and with her new husband, and Alex is also consistently shocked that Daisy isn't the spoiled and dumb socialite that he had pegged her to be. There are a lot of ups and downs, some funny moments, some sexy times, and some sad moments...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between focusing mainly on Daisy and Alex in 3rd person narrative. It did have some parts that focused on side characters as well.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I ate this up and read it super fast! I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No, they take a while to develop stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Alex. I liked him. I felt bad for his past, but I did want him to communicate a little better with Daisy at times.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 5 stars. Daisy. I loved her! She was a mess and a lot lost when we first meet her. Her upbringing and family relationships were sad, but I appreciated the woman she became despite it all.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I teared up a few times, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They both push away and also pursue the relationship at times.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Alright. They have some alright tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story. I do think this could've been a little bit more steamy tbh. Their sexual chemistry just fell a little flat for me for some reason.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ An ex f-buddy of the H is the owner of the circus, and she causes a good bit of drama for the couple (because she had fallen in live with him and he didn't return the feelings). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a descriptive scene of two side characters  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~a month (?), but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Loss of a parent (off page), arranged marriage (on page), child abuse (off page), the h was a virgin, and unexpected pregnancy (on page).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This is my biggest issue with the book. It gives us a small (days?) jump ahead epilogue with some of their HEA, but I definitely wanted more! How about them with their children later in life?! That would've been awesome. I am still calling this a HEA though.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have both the h and H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_3522427996" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3522427996" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3522427996?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6651368-kiss-an-angel">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Arini by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/58714144-tears-of-venus-but-humans-call-me-mina">Tears Of Venus, but humans call me Mina</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3522427996" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1191879426966193212"><b>4.25 Stars</b><br/><br/>We love a man who knows what he wants and go after it, but do you know what I love more?<br/><br/>The sight of grumpy jerkface <b>Alex Markov</b> . . .<br/><br/>↠ getting his heart all twisted up for a woman he realizes too late he’s fallen for; and,<br/>↠ begging on his knees with his ass handed to him because he just got schooled on <i><b>l o v e</b>.</i><br/><br/>Essentially the story involves:<br/><br/>✓ a temporary arranged marriage;<br/>✓ two people who couldn’t be more opposite;<br/>✓ a beautiful love story with sprinkles of drama;<br/>✓ some great character</span>
  <span id="freeText1191879426966193212" style="display:none"><b>4.25 Stars</b><br /><br />We love a man who knows what he wants and go after it, but do you know what I love more?<br /><br />The sight of grumpy jerkface <b>Alex Markov</b> . . .<br /><br />↠ getting his heart all twisted up for a woman he realizes too late he’s fallen for; and,<br />↠ begging on his knees with his ass handed to him because he just got schooled on <i><b>l o v e</b>.</i><br /><br />Essentially the story involves:<br /><br />✓ a temporary arranged marriage;<br />✓ two people who couldn’t be more opposite;<br />✓ a beautiful love story with sprinkles of drama;<br />✓ some great character development;<br />✓ lots of hairy (big and small) animals; and,<br />✓ a circus.<br /><br />You see, Alex is a proud man, cold and aloof. He has preconcieved notions about his wife and doesn’t trust her more than he does a porcupine not to prick you with its sharp quills. He’s awful to her, and he’d be all—<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m not going to fall in love with you, sweetheart. It’s just not going to happen. I care about you, but I don’t love you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Or . . .<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“But I don’t love you, Daisy, and you can’t begin to know how sorry I am about that because if I could choose anyone in this world to love it’d be you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />So, obviously I wasn’t happy he bossed Daisy around, made her do stunts for the carnival, and just being a real bastard. However, on the inside I was also egging him on, like <i>“Yes, you keep treating her like rubbish and let’s see how you feel when you lose her!”</i><br /><br />And boy did he SUFFER.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I don’t love you anymore,” she whispered. “I don’t love you at all.” His throat closed. “It’s all right, sweetheart. I love you enough for both of us.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />I wish there were MORE chapters of him grovelling cause that part was just priceless but also like made me melt. 💗<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I love you, Daisy. I love you so much I hurt.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Best not forget that the <b>real MVP</b> here is <b>Daisy Devreaux</b>.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>His fists clenched at his sides. “Damn it! Where’s your pride?”<br />“Pride? It’s in my heart, of course.”<br />“You’re letting me demean you!”<br />She smiled. “You can’t do that. I can only demean myself.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Vulnerable and insecure, but instead of annoying, it makes her relatable. She’d stand up for herself, let herself fall in love and deal with the consequences, walk away but not without fighting for her marriage first.<br /><br />I have my grievances when it comes to Sheba the ex (like, I don’t need a flashback of her and Alex f*cking or her and Heather’s dad getting it on in the present or her sabotaging the marriage), but ultimately I appreciate how all of the Sheba related drama were resolved.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Daisy’s thoughts after getting tiger back to his cage: That every living being was part of every other living being. That all were part of God. Bound by love. Put on earth to care for one another.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />This was just so wholesome, heart wrenching but also LOL funny and endearing. I loved the circus setting, adored the relationship Daisy developed with the animals and just the overall dynamics among the circus people.<br /><br />The book is mostly about Alex and Daisy, but character growth extends to the side characters as well. <i>Kiss an Angel</i> was published before I was even born, and yet the story and the charm it carries is timeless.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1191879426966193212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_413722446" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/413722446" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/413722446?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=keeper-shelf">keeper-shelf</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer413722446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2280147948916631650"><b>5 BILLION ZILLION GAJILLIONTY STARS</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I take thee... to be my awful wedded husband” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531792461ra/25984296.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I have NO idea how I missed this book by one of my all time favorite authors, considering I've practically read her entire backlist. But I did. And I've been kicking myself for days for taking this long to do it. Because this book? THIS BOOK WAS MAGICAL! It is hands down my favorite contemporary romance, not only from this author, but period. Yes. It was THAT good. Actually, no. It wasn't just good. It w</span>
  <span id="freeText2280147948916631650" style="display:none"><b>5 BILLION ZILLION GAJILLIONTY STARS</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I take thee... to be my awful wedded husband” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531792461ra/25984296.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have NO idea how I missed this book by one of my all time favorite authors, considering I've practically read her entire backlist. But I did. And I've been kicking myself for days for taking this long to do it. Because this book? THIS BOOK WAS MAGICAL! It is hands down my favorite contemporary romance, not only from this author, but period. Yes. It was THAT good. Actually, no. It wasn't just good. It was brilliant. It was enchanting, sigh inducing, heartwarming, funny, swoony, PERFECTION. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">His fists clenched at his sides. “Damn it! Where's your pride?” <br>“Pride? It's in my heart, of course.” <br>“You're letting me demean you!” <br>She smiled. “You can't do that. I can only demean myself.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>If you love the arranged marriage trope, you will LOVE the story of Alex and Daisy. Put against a rock and a hard place, Daisy agrees to her father's choice of husband, even if she's only meets him the day of her wedding. Alex has his own reasons for agreeing to the arrangement, but he's keeping a tight lid on those.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531792461ra/25984297.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Suddenly sweet and somewhat sheltered Daisy that's used to globe trotting and dining with celebrities with her flighty and selfish past model mother, finds herself thrust into circus life, with a husband that's determined to prove to her that she can't hack it. Put to the test on just how much of the ordinary life she can endure, Daisy soon finds that there's something almost magical about the circus, and more than meets the eye to her husband.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531792461ra/25984298.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Daisy was the sweetest, most endearing heroine I've ever read. I loved all of her vulnerabilities and insecurities. I loved her soft sort of strength and the way she finds herself in a place she last expected.<br><br>Alex was an outright bastard to her. Yet there was something so intriguing about him. I couldn't get enough of him. I wanted to hate him for his treatment of Daisy, but then reading about her method of dealing with him gave me too many laughs to care.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Good news!" she chirped. "The doctor says this time it's triplets!” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved the way that Daisy's sweet nature eventually began to win over everyone around her. I loved the incredible cast of quirky and unique secondary characters. My absolute favorite part had to be the animals, though.<br><br>This book was simply EVERYTHING. It was phenomenal, unputdownable, page-turner, smile-inducer. It had THE MOST DELICIOUS GROVEL I have ever read. It had the swooniest romance. It had the quirkiest humor. IT WAS EVERYTHING. EVERYTHING! An absolute must read! My favorite book of the year and hands down my favorite SEP book to date!<br><br><b>Find me on:<br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/DirtyGirlRomance?" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525717.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow me on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://twitter.com/DirtyGrlRomance" target="twitter" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525718.png" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow Me on Twitter" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="http://www.dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436986543i/15525719.png" width="40" height="40" alt="blog" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1530810453i/25928532._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>

<div id="review_985823113" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/985823113" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/985823113?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6972914-karen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer985823113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8966053126092156794"><b>5 STARS</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/poziruy-fine-art-02.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942896._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo poziruy-fine-art-02.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Seriously.. I’m speechless.. LOVE LOVE LOVE this book!!!!</b><br/>It’s official! I am hopelessly in love with Susan Elizabeth Phillips! What a wonderful and endearing story this was. I was glued to the pages from start to finish with a stupid silly grin on my face the whole time. In fact, I can’t help smiling now as I’m writing this review. Just thinking back over the story, makes me want to pick the book up and start in all over again. <br/><br/>The characters were absolutely fantastic. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText8966053126092156794" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/poziruy-fine-art-02.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942896._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo poziruy-fine-art-02.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Seriously.. I’m speechless.. LOVE LOVE LOVE this book!!!!</b><br>It’s official! I am hopelessly in love with Susan Elizabeth Phillips! What a wonderful and endearing story this was. I was glued to the pages from start to finish with a stupid silly grin on my face the whole time. In fact, I can’t help smiling now as I’m writing this review. Just thinking back over the story, makes me want to pick the book up and start in all over again. <br><br>The characters were absolutely fantastic. The dialogue was gritty and romantic with oodles of sexual tension. The supporting characters were just as well developed, even the animals in the circus had me laughing at times and on the edge of my seat at others. The story was so creative and well laid out. I loved everything about it.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women%202/lauren_mellor13.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942897._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo lauren_mellor13.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Theodosia Devreaux (Daisy)</b> is a 26 year old girl with a huge dilemma. She has gotten herself into so much debt that she’s facing jail time. Her wealthy father has offered to help, but has some very unusual demands. She must marry a man her father has chosen for her, and not only does she have to live with him and do as he says, she must stay married for 6 months in order to collect her trust fund. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men2/tumblr_n1i8r5ykoD1r2s83lo6_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942898._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n1i8r5ykoD1r2s83lo6_500.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The bridegroom, <b>Alexander Markov</b>… seems just as unhappy about the arrangement as she does. He may be tall, dark and handsome beyond her wildest dreams… but he’s also angry, brooding and completely incapable of love. And worst of all, he’s determined to show this spoiled little cream puff a long hard lesson in hard living.<br><br><b>
  <i> “I take thee... to be my awful wedded husband” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/tumblr_mhdwibWkUB1r9wyj4o1_1280.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942899._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mhdwibWkUB1r9wyj4o1_1280.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So immediately following this poor excuse for a wedding, Daisy is dragged from her Manhattan lifestyle off to a broken down traveling circus where her new husband is determined to tame her to his ways. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/satc_whip_cracking.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942900.jpg" alt=" photo satc_whip_cracking.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I’m not going to fall in love with you, sweetheart. It’s just not going to happen. I care about you, but I don’t love you.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animals/cfabd507898ac4181ba006149d399685.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942901._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo cfabd507898ac4181ba006149d399685.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Daisy is completely out of her element. She is immediately treated like an outsider by all of the circus staff, she is terrified of animals, and has discovered that her scary new husband is an expert with bull whips… and he’s not above threatening her with retaliation if she defy’s him. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/ROTLA_whip12.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425428061i/13888766._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo ROTLA_whip12.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh, and to top it all off… Daisy soon finds that her Alex has quite the reputation with women. And upon finding him married, they quickly turn their backs on her, making her the pariah of the circus.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/hc-circus-in-winter-chester-1023-20141016-001.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942902.jpg" alt=" photo hc-circus-in-winter-chester-1023-20141016-001.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But, Daisy isn’t going to let this defeat her. She is determined to see this commitment through. And finding a few cracks in his angry facade, Daisy soon finds herself feeling empathy for Alex. Empathy that soon starts feeling something like love. <br><br><b>
  <i>“His fists clenched at his sides. 'Damn it! Where's your pride?' <br>'Pride? It's in my heart, of course.' <br>'You're letting me demean you!' <br>She smiled. 'You can't do that. I can only demean myself.” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/5089c9c84e1ae674b735b3e92ac0f201.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942903._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5089c9c84e1ae674b735b3e92ac0f201.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Although, even as she offers him her heart, he completely shuts her out, until she is finally convinced that he will never love her. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I don't love you anymore", she whispered. "I don't love you at all." His throat closed. "It's all right, sweetheart. I love you enough for both of us.”</i>
</b><br><br>I just cannot say enough about this book. I LOVED Daisy!!! She was sweet and loving, but also spunky and stubborn. She was put in a horrible situation and instead of giving up and falling to despair, she turned out to be a beacon of light that brought life back into the circus. Not only did she prove to herself that she was made of tougher stuff, she also inspired everyone around her, including the man that was determined to break her. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/725ef7bd3f3722784f4aa73cd54e63a0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425857227i/13942951._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 725ef7bd3f3722784f4aa73cd54e63a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “You shouldn’t dare a person who doesn’t have anything left to lose.”</i>
</b><br><br>And Alex… well here is a guy you will not soon forget. A real top-rank ass with an ego that was bigger than the big-top tent. A real alpha maniac, who thought quite a lot of himself, while showing little regard for the fairer sex… especially empty-headed, spoiled brat socialites that took advantage of their family’s fortune. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/Oxeye-daisy-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425857228i/13942952._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Oxeye-daisy-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I can’t resist you,” he said quietly. “You know that, don’t you? And I’m tired of pretending I can.” His expression grew more troubled. “But I don’t love you, Daisy, and you can’t begin to know how sorry I am about that because if I could chose anyone in this world to love, it’d be you.”</i>
</b> <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animals/l-Baby-Elephant_1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425857228i/13942953._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo l-Baby-Elephant_1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it didn’t take long for Daisy to start melting the ice surrounding Alex Markov’s heart. <br>And while he felt himself damaged and incapable of love, Alex soon found he was finding it harder and harder to stay away from girl he thought was beyond help. <br><br><b>
  <i>She wasn’t holding anything back. Not one thing. She was offering herself without reservations: heart, body, and soul. How could anyone be so self-destructive? He pulled himself back together. If she wasn’t going to guard herself, he’d do the job for her.</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects2/shutterstock_642371202-670x476.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425857228i/13942954._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo shutterstock_642371202-670x476.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I love you, Daisy. I love you so much I hurt.”</i>
</b><br><br>This is such a delightful story. And the circus setting made it that much more endearing. The animals themselves played their parts to perfection, and in doing so, helped Daisy find her way in life. These new relationships were so touching, it will make your hear ache with joy. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Animals/8387f6596fe0fe260f05cf388b8d2713.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425856700i/13942904._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8387f6596fe0fe260f05cf388b8d2713.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>While they kissed, Tater dusted both of them with hay, just as if he thought the stuff was rice.</i>
</b><br><br>I highly recommend this book!!! And a big thank you to Ingela and Mo who recommended it to me. ❤︎</span>
  <a data-text-id="8966053126092156794" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_550613819" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550613819" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550613819?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=married-couple">married-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=strong-willed-heroine">strong-willed-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=deliciously-sweet">deliciously-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-secondary-characters">wonderful-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=passionate">passionate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=overcoming-tragedy">overcoming-tragedy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550613819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11573374879001057229"><br/>Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>4 1/2 Fun time Stars!! I didn't just love this book; I'm in love with it!!</b><br/><br/>Admittedly when I started to read this I thought this was not going to work for me. Boy was I ever wrong!!! Even with the over-the-top unrealistic circumstances that surrounded the characters, this book <b>STOLE MY HEART!!</b> Daisy, oh my goodness, talk about wearing your heart on your sleeve, she did everything… everything out of love!! She was one of the sweetest, kindest, most determined</span>
  <span id="freeText11573374879001057229" style="display:none"><br />Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>4 1/2 Fun time Stars!! I didn't just love this book; I'm in love with it!!</b><br /><br />Admittedly when I started to read this I thought this was not going to work for me. Boy was I ever wrong!!! Even with the over-the-top unrealistic circumstances that surrounded the characters, this book <b>STOLE MY HEART!!</b> Daisy, oh my goodness, talk about wearing your heart on your sleeve, she did everything… everything out of love!! She was one of the sweetest, kindest, most determined heroines I've ever had the good fortune to come across! I adored her, and just thinking about her now just warms my heart. <br /><br />Thrown into circumstances she's totally unprepared for, Daisy makes the best of the situation. She finds herself married to the cold-hearted, yet devastatingly handsome Alexander Markov. He throws every obstacle he can at her, but she is determined, keeps her chin up and pushes through. I was fascinated by her, she was delightful! I did not like Alex at first, but as Daisy works her magic and he starts to come around, she falls for him and so did I. Alex was carrying around some heavy baggage and he built a fortress around himself and his heart, but Daisy is so damn irresistible that his walls begin to crumble ever so slowly. He puts up a great front, but the reader can feel how much he cares for this woman who shares his bed and his life. The deal for the marriage calls for 6 months, but how can he ever let her go?! Her father and step-mother, I don’t even want to talk about them, they’re not worth the effort…<b>BLECH!</b><br /><br />Hear that crack?!?! It’s my heart breaking in half and it wasn’t the only thing cracking and well…you’ll just have to read it and see for yourself!! <b>OMG</b>…even now it all just takes my breath away, my heart pounds and I’m anxious all over again. It was a defining moment in the book and I can’t say any more than that! <br /><br />The ending took me totally off guard. I never expected it to play out the way it did. It was such a pleasant surprise, my jaw just dropped to the floor and it took a while for me to lift it up and put it back in place. I read the last 12% of this book over and over…I had a hard time putting this one away. <br /><br />So many amazing characters that took front and center, but the two that stole the show were Sinjun and Tater! Their special relationship with Daisy, well it was just that…<b>SPECIAL!</b> However unrealistic it was, it worked in a big way. <br /><br />So much fun, SEP outdid herself with this one. This book stirred every emotion in me…it was head-spinning! The dialogue was amazing; I was captivated by the story and charmed by all the characters, especially Daisy and Alex. The passion they shared felt real and they had amazing chemistry. SEP does intimate very well. The book was not lacking for heat, that’s for sure. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Kiss An Angel </i>
</b>is now a comfort read on my shelf; I can pull this out anytime and know that it will leave me feeling good, and that’s saying something!!! I can’t recommend this book enough!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11573374879001057229" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer705404532787414095">+++2 stars only for the writing+++<br/><br/>I still cant fully decide how im feeling about this book. First i want to say that when i first started this book i thought that its not what i expected because of that cover, i thought that it really needed a change because it was quite good, <b>BUT</b> than i found out that this book definitely doesnt need a different cover, its really what you can see in that picture - stupid naive pathetic little girl who lets people walk over her through the whole freakin book.<br/>She</span>
  <span id="freeText705404532787414095" style="display:none">+++2 stars only for the writing+++<br><br>I still cant fully decide how im feeling about this book. First i want to say that when i first started this book i thought that its not what i expected because of that cover, i thought that it really needed a change because it was quite good, <b>BUT</b> than i found out that this book definitely doesnt need a different cover, its really what you can see in that picture - stupid naive pathetic little girl who lets people walk over her through the whole freakin book.<br>She was manipulated so often i was pulling my hair out. Literally.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458360045ra/18478776.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It starts when our heroine Daisy is forced to marry this circus asshole Alex.<br>The plot is very simple. Its something like that:<br><br>Naive and Dickhead get married. <br>Naive hopes that D will fall in love with her.<br>Dickhead tells N that he isnt capable of love.<br>Dickhead humiliates N all the time so of course she falls in love with him.<br>Dickhead remindes N that he cant love her.<br>Dickhead humiliates N again.<br>Naive loves D even more.<br>Its 80% of book.<br>Dickhead is still being dickhead.<br>Naive finally founds her backbone and runs!<br>Dickhead goes after her and what the fuck does Naive? She fucking comes back to him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388736951ra/7912859.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And they live their HEA.<br><br>What is even worse? After all, you expect "hero" to grovel. He didnt, not even a little bit. I cant even express how angry i was after i finished this, but it was similar to this<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398903006ra/9480455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just wanted to punch him so badly...<br><br>It was one of those books where i wished so much for the heroine to leave, find someone normal, fall in love and live with this OM happily ever after. And for hero to watch it all and be miserable for the rest of his life.<br><br>Only plus i would say was scenes with animals, thats all i enjoyed, but the rest i was mostly skipping, mainly all those circus perfomances, they were too long and boring. So no, i wont be re-reading this book. <br><br><b>I would recommend this to anyone who is looking for book where:</b><br><br>- heroine is embarrassed and humiliated the whole book<br>- heroine is pathetic doormat <br>- hero who is so much asshole that you will need absolutely new shelv for him<br>- hero who continued flirting with OW even when he was married - i dont care that it was forced marriage i still consider it as cheating, i bet if the heroine didnt always cut it off it would continue somewhere private<br>- dumb OW drama<br>- hero who doesnt grovel after being dickhead 80% of book<br>- when hero rapes the heroine, some may argue with me but i still think it was rape, hero admitted it too<br><br>SAFETY:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Heroine is virgin, saving herself for marriage.<br>Hero had his share of woman.<br>OW drama lama. Also had descriptive sexual detailes in flashbacks with this OW.<br>No OM.<br>They didnt used condoms.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9326632592275111703"><b>KISS AN ANGEL</b> published 18 years ago<br/><br/><b>Daisy</b> has finally pushed her dad to his breaking point. Spending all her deceased mother’s money and racking up debt has lead her father to give her one last chance. This last chance involves marrying a stranger and staying “happily” married to him for 6 months which after her time is up she can divorce him and collect a trust fund. Sounds easy enough?!?!<br/><br/><b>Alex</b> is a strict Russian who has agreed to marry Daisy because of a debt he owes her father. To break Daisy</span>
  <span id="freeText9326632592275111703" style="display:none"><b>KISS AN ANGEL</b> published 18 years ago<br><br><b>Daisy</b> has finally pushed her dad to his breaking point. Spending all her deceased mother’s money and racking up debt has lead her father to give her one last chance. This last chance involves marrying a stranger and staying “happily” married to him for 6 months which after her time is up she can divorce him and collect a trust fund. Sounds easy enough?!?!<br><br><b>Alex</b> is a strict Russian who has agreed to marry Daisy because of a debt he owes her father. To break Daisy of her wild and frivolous ways he’s been informed that he must be firm when dealing with her. Alex is a no nonsense man who manages a traveling circus. <br><br>The circus atmosphere along with the animals adds to the completeness of the story. <b> I really want my own <i>Sinjuin the tiger.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390164437i/8155549._SX540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Standalone</b><br><br> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_challenges/1196247" rel="nofollow noopener">10th book of 2014</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610049373" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7968269302996448476"><b>5 Stars once again </b><br/><br/>July 8, 2020 ~ Reread ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️<br/><br/>This time I was listening to the audiobook narrated by the very best <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/62817.Anna_Fields' title='Anna Fields' rel='nofollow noopener'>Anna Fields</a>. Love this wonderful romance.   <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <a href='http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>I'm in love! In love... </b>In this wonderful story. Therefore, this</span>
  <span id="freeText7968269302996448476" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars once again </b><br><br>July 8, 2020 ~ Reread ❤️❤️❤️❤️❤️<br><br>This time I was listening to the audiobook narrated by the very best <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/62817.Anna_Fields" title="Anna Fields" rel="nofollow noopener">Anna Fields</a>. Love this wonderful romance. Maybe the best by SEP.<br><br>I LIKE - ... and love <br>😘 ………………… 😘<br><br><i>Written September 14, 2013</i><br><br><b>5 Glimmering Huge Stars - Amazing, wonderful, sentimental, romantic... just the best kind of romance - simply a story that must be read - and now belongs to my top shelf</b><br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I'm in love! In love... </b>In this wonderful story. Therefore, this is an exuberant, completely one-sided tribute review and must be read with an ounce of sanity. Because I never want to stop and will say again and again in different ways how much I love this book. Please be patient!! <br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>
  <i>Welcome to the Circus!</i>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Books/6d5e7b19-6352-4f7b-ac14-7642a2d367c8_zps1179e0b4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420792i/835155.jpg" alt=" photo 6d5e7b19-6352-4f7b-ac14-7642a2d367c8_zps1179e0b4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br>I just want to scream - <b>What a great novel!!</b> I'm so impressed, almost 20 years old (written 1996) but it outperforms most in the genre even though it is in a traditional romance style. Maybe nothing new under the sun but in this case it doesn't hurt. I don't think you get a story who is in anyway hyped, vulgar, to sugar sweet or overly fuss to keep us, the readers, on the rack - you just get a good well thought out story. Sure it's steamy with a very hot, handsome alpha hero (Alex, you are a favorite!). There is both happiness, tears, laughter but above all an <b>absolutely incredible wonderful heroine</b> in the lovely Daisy (an angel is really the right term). When it comes down to it, it's mostly novels <b>with a heroine I really can love</b> who will also be the most memorable in the long run. <br><br><b>No doubt; highest rating!</b><br><blockquote>‘She dug her nails into her palms and told herself she had no choice. "I, Theodosia..." She gulped for air. "...take thee Alexander..." She gulped again. "...to be my awful wedded husband...” </blockquote><br><b>Daisy Devreaux</b> can either go to jail or marry <b>Alex Markov</b>, the man her father has chosen for her. Arranged marriages in a contemporary romance? Yes, poor Daisy have debts and her father has a condition to help her. She, his daughter, must be married to, and live as wife, with the stranger man her father picked out in six months. When the time has elapsed, they may go separate paths and Daisy will get access to a trust fund and can choose how she wants to live her life. <br><br>What do you do as a 26 year old woman with debt and without a job? - folds up to fate...<br><blockquote>“Don't dare a person who has nothing else left to lose.” <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Books/image_zpsd2b456c9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420792i/835156.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsd2b456c9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>Just a few minutes after the wedding</b> drags Daisy from her NY life to the airport. A few hours later, they're in Florida and she faces that her new married life to a stranger is going to be with a traveling second class circus. Her new husband is nasty, lasting, superior and menacing and is pointing to a mangy old-fashioned caravan; her new home. As if that were not bad enough, Daisy is terrified of animals...<br><blockquote>“Well alright then," His eyes glittered. "I get my kicks whipping woman I have sex with and you're next on my list. Now I'm going to take a shower.” <br>~ ~ <br>“What are you gonna do, angel face? Stab me with your eyebrow pencil?” </blockquote><br><b>There is so much to tell</b>. Here are a lot of lovely second characters and their stories. We have the charmer Brady, the bitter but so tough Sheba and the young insecure teenager Heather. It is whining whips, horse arts and one for me quite new and unknown circus world. It's humble, lives in mobile homes, muddy, constant travel, much gossip and bullshit, but also caring and warmth.<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Books/image_zps84991f30.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420792i/835157.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps84991f30.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘... the troublesome baby elepahant, the shy gorilla, the old, reagal tiger.’</blockquote><br><b>Very important was also all the animals</b>. Tater the baby elephant in love, Glenna a lonely female gorilla and of course the poor old "talking" tiger Sinjun. Animals in cramped cages and with rather dire living conditions which Daisy came to take care of and started to love. I really liked that part of the story and I'm barely even an animal lover. <br><br><b>But above all it was the love.</b> The love between two very different people, with different backgrounds and ways to show emotions. One gave us everything. Her heart was open to everybody, animals like humans. The other one had long since lost his. He could no longer love. <br><br>First there was wrangling, viciousness, fuss and digs. Then came the attraction and heat. Then acceptens, friendship - but could it be love? Sometimes I was so mad at Alex. He was so unfair, stubborn and stuck in his old beliefs. I almost cried after getting this <u>three</u> so, by me and by Daisy, awaited and needed beautiful words. <i>I Love You.</i> ...just say them, please.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Books/image_zpse1b984c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420792i/835158.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpse1b984c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>My heart hoped, was torn apart</b>, healed and became contented. It was an ordeal to get through. But a good one which was awarded.<br><blockquote>“You foolish man. Of course there's love. Don't you know? I love you.” </blockquote><br><b>As you already understood; I LOVED it</b>. I loved Daisy and Alex, their grand lovestory, their friends and all the cute animals in the circus. Yes the whole thing! Beautifully told, entertaining, very funny and enjoyable to read and of course super romantic. <br><br>There are good and there are better novels - GREAT novels. This book definitely belongs to the group for the better, the great ones. For me is it unforgettable one. A story I know I will read again.... and that doesn't happen every day. <br><br>Big <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/t-kiss.php" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392582839ra/8580626.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I LIKE - hauntingly good - a real romance</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7968269302996448476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer13751030241859144791"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/>My first SEP novel and it was oh soooo good!!!! Normally contemporary romance novels from the 90's aren't really my thing, but this was compared to The Unwanted Wife by Natasha Anders so I had to read it.<br/><br/>Kiss An Angel is the story of Daisy who gets roped into an arranged marriage to a man who seems to despise her. Alex works for a traveling circus and seems to find a lot of pleasure in assigning Daisy to tasks which would humiliate her. As time goes by, sparks fly between the two and</span>
  <span id="freeText13751030241859144791" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br>My first SEP novel and it was oh soooo good!!!! Normally contemporary romance novels from the 90's aren't really my thing, but this was compared to The Unwanted Wife by Natasha Anders so I had to read it.<br><br>Kiss An Angel is the story of Daisy who gets roped into an arranged marriage to a man who seems to despise her. Alex works for a traveling circus and seems to find a lot of pleasure in assigning Daisy to tasks which would humiliate her. As time goes by, sparks fly between the two and they give in to their attraction. But Alex will never love anyone, and he makes it clear he will never love Daisy.<br><br>This book started out a bit rough for me, I almost threw in the towel and I pushed on. I'm so glad I did because after 20% or so I was unable to put down this book. Then 70% hit and it was angsty AF so of course I was vomiting happy rainbows out of my mouth. I'm such an angst whore, I swear. I really liked Daisy and Alex, I liked them even more together. Another highlight for me was the relationships developed with the circus animals because I am a giant softy for animals.<br><br>I cannot wait to discover more by SEP!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥</span>
