<div id="review_1624104432" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1624104432" />
    <a title="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19958389-christina-brunette-reader"><img alt="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532563583p2/19958389.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1624104432?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christina ~ Brunette Reader" href="/user/show/19958389-christina-brunette-reader">Christina ~ Brunette Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19958389-christina-brunette-reader?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19958389-christina-brunette-reader?shelf=frankly-my-dear">frankly-my-dear</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19958389-christina-brunette-reader?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1624104432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10684734222543425023"><br/>It's not long, about few months, since I've luckily discovered SEP's books and after having enjoyed, more or less, all the other eight I've read so far, I can safely say that with <i>Kiss an Angel</i> I've found my first and only big disappointment. I am aware this is a rather widely beloved classic of the genre and of her backlist, and I can even see why to a certain extent, but I guess I'll have to take my turn at "unpopular opinion time" in this case. There are copious great reviews already covering</span>
  <span id="freeText10684734222543425023" style="display:none"><br />It's not long, about few months, since I've luckily discovered SEP's books and after having enjoyed, more or less, all the other eight I've read so far, I can safely say that with <i>Kiss an Angel</i> I've found my first and only big disappointment. I am aware this is a rather widely beloved classic of the genre and of her backlist, and I can even see why to a certain extent, but I guess I'll have to take my turn at "unpopular opinion time" in this case. There are copious great reviews already covering both ends of the scale, so I won't delve into the plot and details and just explain why this story really didn't work for me.<br /><br />Despite being a vintage release (1996), the narrative style was crisp and engaging as ever, the dialogues infused with humour and, like the lovely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73084.Heaven__Texas__Chicago_Stars___2_" title="Heaven, Texas (Chicago Stars, #2) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Heaven, Texas</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9292809.Lady_Be_Good__Wynette__Texas___2_" title="Lady Be Good (Wynette, Texas, #2) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Be Good</a>, written around the same years, the book didn't feel dated at all in that regard. My gripes stem from elsewhere, namely the over-the-top storyline and, even more so, the romance between the leads, Daisy Devreaux and Alex Markov. <br /><br />In fact, I couldn't stand Alex, right from the beginning to the very end. <br /><br />There, I said it.<br /><br />When encountering such exceptionally good writing, I usually tend to have more patience with overdone characterisations and circumstances, but this time the outlandish premise set in motion by Daisy's hateful father and the hero's retrograde attitude were just too much to pass. Alex belongs to an old-school bodice ripper, possibly taking place no later than the 18th Century (hey, some of those Victorian guys could be very forward-thinking compared to our hero here!), but in a contemporary context his arrogant behaviour toward a woman who has done him absolutely no wrong to boot, felt so irritating and off-putting as to ruin my whole reading experience. His troubled past is no excuse and till the very last page he acted as if he knew what was best for Daisy in a selfish and dramatic attempt to clean his conscience instead. <br />As for Daisy, while spending entire portions of the book alternatively being overwhelmed by him or justifying his actions, she crossed the line between "accommodating" and "doormat" one time too many, and her naively cheerful disposition more often than not seemed like passivity covered by a thick layer of forced optimism, a type of heroine I'm totally incapable to relate to.<br />At the end she sounded so drained and resigned, like anybody would if put through the emotional wringer by an uncaring partner, that letting the self-important windbag have his way and shut up and be done with it started to look like an option. Not my idea of romance at all.<br /><br />The itinerant circus setting was well-portrayed and original, but even the secondary characters were mostly exaggerated stereotypes, like Sheba, the "strong" woman of the situation, and the quasi-preternatural connection Daisy develops with some animals further detracted from my enjoyment, since I usually don't care for unexpected paranormal abilities popping up to show a character's specialness in what is initially presented as a realistic background, especially when contemporary.<br />If I don't regret having read this book, for the always delicious writing, the fast moving plot and a little bit for having finally slaked my curiosity, I can't see myself picking it up ever again, nor would I recommend beginning one's acquaintance with SEP's oeuvre from here. At the risk of repeating myself always bringing him up as an absolute paragon, Heath, the hero from her irresistible <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73089.Match_Me_If_You_Can__Chicago_Stars___6_" title="Match Me If You Can (Chicago Stars, #6) by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Match Me If You Can</a>, is worth ten Alex Markovs (and maybe some more).<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10684734222543425023" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1624104432">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1220299452" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8145370802074631321">It has been a lazy day for me. I didn’t do much other than read and lounge outside in the sun. So I am going to continue with my laziness and provide you with a short and sweet review. <br/><br/>Susan Elizabeth Phillips rocks! Now that I have read and loved enough of her books I have put her on the dreaded author pedestal. I know I shouldn’t but I have and thankfully I absolutely adored <b>Kiss an Angel</b> from start to finish. <br/><br/>I won’t go on and on about the characters or the plot simply because there are a few</span>
  <span id="freeText8145370802074631321" style="display:none">It has been a lazy day for me. I didn’t do much other than read and lounge outside in the sun. So I am going to continue with my laziness and provide you with a short and sweet review. <br /><br />Susan Elizabeth Phillips rocks! Now that I have read and loved enough of her books I have put her on the dreaded author pedestal. I know I shouldn’t but I have and thankfully I absolutely adored <b>Kiss an Angel</b> from start to finish. <br /><br />I won’t go on and on about the characters or the plot simply because there are a few FANTASTIC reviews written by Karen, Angela and Ingela that you must check out if you haven’t already. Their words are spot on and their pictures capture some of my favorite moments in the book too.<br /><br />But I will say…..<br /><br />The two main characters Daisy and Alex were pretty amazing. The moments between them were endless. There was humor, sweetness and sexiness. ❤ And one thing I always love about SEP books are the side story and side characters. In this one, SEP had me falling for a baby elephant named Tater and a Siberian Tiger named Sinjun. <br /><br />The plot was creative and filled with SEP originality. The candidness of the dialogue was perfect. It provided for laughter, romance and endless sexual tension. Which I must say I loved! As the story starts to peak I found myself completely invested in not only Daisy and Alex’s love story but the relationships of the others characters. It really was a wonderful story.<br /><br />While my favorite SEP books are her Chicago Star’s Series, I highly recommend this one too! <br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1279200562" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6055324907551229713"><b>UPDATE: Reducing stars from my original million of stars rating because my taste in romance has changed, because safety issues and because NOT ENOUGH GROVELING. </b> <br/><br/>UNSAFE READ ALERT<br/>UNSAFE READ ALERT<br/><br/><b> Rape/dubious consent </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[In My humble opinion and I don't expect everyone to see it the same way I do, the consent is dubious all through out the book. For starters because neither of them want to be married to each other. For me it's clear H and h want each other badly and it might seem th</span></span>
  <span id="freeText6055324907551229713" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE: Reducing stars from my original million of stars rating because my taste in romance has changed, because safety issues and because NOT ENOUGH GROVELING. </b> <br /><br />UNSAFE READ ALERT<br />UNSAFE READ ALERT<br /><br /><b> Rape/dubious consent </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[In My humble opinion and I don't expect everyone to see it the same way I do, the consent is dubious all through out the book. For starters because neither of them want to be married to each other. For me it's clear H and h want each other badly and it might seem that all sex was consensual, but there are several consent issues here, that go beyond the sex because this couple was forced to marriage and manipulated to have sex in order to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ produce a heir and I can't blame Alexander for getting angry, I just wish he had gotten angry at his idiotic father in law, not a Daisy, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I didn't find it blatantly rapist, because the way it's written it makes me feel as though they want each other and agree to the sex, but I'd be careful with this one if dubious consent is your trigger. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>CHEATING: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Techically not, but here's the thing: After H and h have kissed and have sex, Alexander is still fliriting with other women. I prefer heroes who have eyes only for the heroine. Besides she was taking her wedding vows seriously and he knew it, so he should have been respectful. I didn't hate it that much because this flirting with OW was used to give Daisy very funny lines. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b> OW= Othe woman: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Graphic sex scene with OW. It's not at present time,<br /> it was part of the heroe's flashback of the time when he was a teen. Now several decades later he still works with OW and he even teams up with her to punish Daisy for something she didn't do. Because he trusts this woman he has known for decades more than he trusts his wife he has been with for only a month <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>HEA </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes, but it came withot enough groveling IMHO  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />In spite of this issues know I'll re-read in the future because:<br /><br />1) Excellent writing and character development. All the characters are well-written. You may love them, you may hate them, but all of them are compelling and true to themselves. All of them, including the bullied teen, Heather move in a rather grey zone. They aren't totally innocent or totally evil.<br /><br />2) DAISY MARKOV is still one of my favorite heroines ever! She's not a doormat, or at least I can't see her that way after so many re-reads. Why? Because this is my personal opinion: <b>WOMEN WHO TAKE THEIR WEDDING VOWS SERIOUSLY AND TRY HARD TO SAVE THEIR MARRIAGES (Knowing well their own limits) AREN'T DOORMATS THEY ARE STRONG</b>. But I can see why so many people in this modern world where couple divorce when their romantic/sexual expectations aren't met would see Daisy efforts as weak, specially after the "accidental" physical abuse. (More on that tomorrow, when I'm ready to write more about this subject) I'll only say: To each their own. <br /><br />3) This is still as addictive as I remember. Once I started I couldn't put it down and I hated every moment I had to stop reading.<br /><br />4) The animals! Sinjun and Tater! I love how Daisy found herself thanks to the animals and the danger and cuteness of her interactions with them is amazing. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br />So what is this book about?<br />The book opers rather strong, the heroine, Daisy, is getting married to a total stranger and she can't even remember his name when it's her turn to say her vows. Isn't that cool? The said stranger takes her to the rural side of the USA to the circus where he's determined to break his wife and make her see she's not cut for his life. Except that Daisy is taking her marriage vows seriously and won't go away without a fight.<br /><br />Is this abusive? Totally, but I admire Daisy strength. I'll write more on this later as my lunch hour is over.<br /><br />MORE TO COME!<br /><br /><br />****<br />***<br /><br /><br /><b> Original review </b><br />Oh Alex! I didn't know what to expect from this book and I'm not dissapointed. I highly recommend this one to every one who loves contemporary romance.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118991281" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9442541805120799093"><b> 5++++ Stars Contemporary Romance </b><br/><br/>This is the third time I have read this book, and I would have to say that the story of Alex and Daisy never gets old. Its a beautiful love story with a strong cast of characters, each playing a vital role to make this story a worthwhile read.<br/><br/>Alex Markov was rescued by Daisy’s father Max when he was twelve years old from the constant physical abuse he was facing under his uncle Sergey. Max had bought Alex from his uncle and seen to his education. Alex had shaped</span>
  <span id="freeText9442541805120799093" style="display:none"><b> 5++++ Stars Contemporary Romance </b><br /><br />This is the third time I have read this book, and I would have to say that the story of Alex and Daisy never gets old. Its a beautiful love story with a strong cast of characters, each playing a vital role to make this story a worthwhile read.<br /><br />Alex Markov was rescued by Daisy’s father Max when he was twelve years old from the constant physical abuse he was facing under his uncle Sergey. Max had bought Alex from his uncle and seen to his education. Alex had shaped into a cold, aloof man who has a strong sense of honor and pride which he holds onto with his life.<br /><br />Daisy is the direct opposite of Alex. An illegitimate child, the only mistake her diplomat father had made in his entire life, Daisy had lived her whole life trying to gain the approval of a father who has never really seen what a remarkable woman Daisy had turned into, regardless of the promiscuous lifestyle Daisy’s beautiful mother had subjected her to. Vulnerable, kind and easy going to a fault, Daisy’s father considers her to be a fluffy scatterbrained individual whom he arranges to be married to Alex for a period of six months. Broke without a dollar to her name, Daisy has no choice but to go ahead with the marriage or face prison for maxing out her credit cards and finding all the creditors after her, the result of shopping extravagantly to make up for the profound sense of loneliness she has been feeling since her mother died.<br /><br />Alex thinks no better of Daisy than her father and vows to give her a fair chance to work through the temporary arrangement which Alex has agreed to with Max. Alex introduces Daisy to the life of living and working in a circus, and for someone like Daisy who has a perpetual fear of animals this doesn’t prove to be an easy feat. With a husband who doesn’t want to have to do anything with her except grudgingly acknowledge the intense feelings of passion that Daisy is able to arouse in him, Daisy finds herself unprepared for what is about to hit her.<br /><br />Alex doesn’t trust his wife one bit and when she is framed as a thief, Alex serves her with the sentence of cleaning up the muck of the animal stalls at the circus. Daisy proves she has a backbone of steel when with determination she surpasses everyone’s expectations of her by sticking to her punishment regardless of the fact she is innocent of the crime.<br /><br />Regardless of the cold layer of indifference Alex tries to put up with, he soon finds himself intrigued with his new wife, whilst Daisy slowly teaches Alex how to care, love and share with his better half.<br /><br />Things get interesting when Daisy gets pregnant, something which Alex had made Daisy swear she would take all the necessary precautions against. In a moment of anger, Alex loses the woman he only realizes too late that he has fallen for, and the lengths Alex has to go through to win Daisy’s love back would touch any romantics heart.<br /><br />The author is known for her talent in weaving a romantic tale filled with laugh aloud moments together with moments of intense passion that makes this book one worth re-reading from time to time. I highly recommend this book to anyone who loves a good romance. Am sure that you wouldn’t be disappointed!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9442541805120799093" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884939188?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zakirrah BookBlogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zakirrah BookBlogger" href="/user/show/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger">Zakirrah BookBlogger</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15894726-zakirrah-bookblogger?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884939188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8597355356192167975"><b>5 Brilliant, Beautiful, Amazing Stars! </b><br/><br/>Okay I bloody loved this book! It was just amazing and I know that I will deffo be re-reading this one day because that's how good it was..Anddd into my favourites it goes ;) <br/><br/>Do you want a funny yet moving, gripping, awesome read? Yeah? <b>GO READ THIS BOOK NOW! :D</b><br/><br/>I loved how different this book was to the normal cliche books I seem to keep picking up.this book evoked emotion, laughter, joy, sadness and much more.I was taken on a journey and I got lost in the </span>
  <span id="freeText8597355356192167975" style="display:none"><b>5 Brilliant, Beautiful, Amazing Stars! </b><br><br>Okay I bloody loved this book! It was just amazing and I know that I will deffo be re-reading this one day because that's how good it was..Anddd into my favourites it goes ;) <br><br>Do you want a funny yet moving, gripping, awesome read? Yeah? <b>GO READ THIS BOOK NOW! :D</b><br><br>I loved how different this book was to the normal cliche books I seem to keep picking up.this book evoked emotion, laughter, joy, sadness and much more.I was taken on a journey and I got lost in the pages, I lived and wanted to stay in this book forever. The magical setting of a circus was brilliant and I am so glad I read this book!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395337192i/8981643.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You meet Daisy and find out that she is getting married to someone she hasn't met..She doesn't want to get married but her father has had enough of her and forces her to get married to a man he picked out.Its basically an arrangement which her father has set up. She goes along with it as she doesn't have any money to do anything else and he believes she owes him.When you first meet Alex I was like eh? wait is he going to be the main character? wow I didn't know what to think or expect.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>‘She dug her nails into her palms and told herself she had no choice. "I, Theodosia..." She gulped for air. "...take thee Alexander..." She gulped again. "...to be my awful wedded husband...”</b>
</i><br><br><br>Daisy thinks she can get out of the arrangement which is for 6 months, if she leaves Alex before that time her father will have nothing to do with her and she wont have any money to do anything.Deciding that the only way out is to make a deal with her so called husband who treats her like a spoiled brat.He pays half the money her father paid him for marriage and they go their own ways and her father wouldn't know anything.That plan fails when he declines and they end up at the circus.<br><br><b>
  <i>"We can do this easy, or we can do it rough. Either way, I'm going to win. You decide how it'll be."</i>
</b><br><br>Alex is such an arsehole at times but his comments made me laugh, his past made me want to squeeze him and never let go.He is hard on Daisy , pushing her way beyond her limits and trying to make her crack.the quicker she understands she can't handle being with him the easier it would be on Alex.For him the marriage isn't a real marriage just an arrangement, just a favour and nothing more.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Well alright then," His eyes glittered. "I get my kicks whipping woman I have sex with and you're next on my list. Now I'm going to take a shower.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395342462i/8982436._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Daisy has always seen marriage as a sacred bond and she is willing to make this work no matter how much Alex pushes her, she is strong, stubborn and won't give up that easily.I love their bickering and how amusing they were.Being with Alex changes Daisy for the better he pushes her makes her work hard, feel confident and stronger.<br><br>Daisy is perfect for Alex, someone who feels he can't love due to his past.She is loving, caring and patient with him, she is the opposite of him and that works, he needs someone soft and caring rather than strong willed, arrogant and well you know..too much like him! I Love love loved Alex! I want more, I really didn't want it to end and I couldn't stop reading,I was up late at night totally captured by this book.<br><br> <i> <b>“I don't love you anymore", she whispered. "I don't love you at all." His throat closed. "It's all right, sweetheart. I love you enough for both of us.”</b></i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395344024ra/8982676.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396289243i/9111686.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh and how could I forget the amazing animals who have their own place in my heart! I loved all the animals (I just realised I missed out the gorilla damn it!) they represented many of the characters in a way, they were caged whether it was by their pride, their greed or their loved ones. Lots of the characters like the animals were lonely all they needed was one person to look at them differently, to care about then, to see them and love them.<br><br>This was my first SEP book and it definitely wont be my last!<br><br><br><i>Check out my blog for more reviews!<br><br>Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/">http://zakirrahsbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/</a><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/ZakirrahsBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/ZakirrahsBoo...</a><br>Twitter:<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/ZBookBlog">https://twitter.com/ZBookBlog</a></i></span>

    <a title="Lady Heather " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2736715-lady-heather"><img alt="Lady Heather " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1418473645p2/2736715.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/551264878?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Heather " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Heather " href="/user/show/2736715-lady-heather">Lady Heather </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6651368-kiss-an-angel">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">contemporary romance</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=broken-women-finding-their-hea">broken-women-finding-their-hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=my-virgin-read-of-this-author">my-virgin-read-of-this-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=domineering-alpha-lead">domineering-alpha-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2736715-lady-heather?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551264878" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10494894150896969345"><br/>I finished this book late last night because: <br/><br/>a) I couldn't put it down, and <br/>b) I had to see if Alex would finally redeem himself after being such a selfish shit!<br/><br/>... needless to say that all is well in the land of HEA's, and I was finally able to sleep after a rather gut-wretching, nerve-wracking, nail-biting reading experience...*yay*.. just the type of book I needed to read!<br/><br/>I don't think the author could have written a more despicable, cold, and hateful character. Alex Markov was so wrapped up</span>
  <span id="freeText10494894150896969345" style="display:none"><br>I finished this book late last night because: <br><br>a) I couldn't put it down, and <br>b) I had to see if Alex would finally redeem himself after being such a selfish shit!<br><br>... needless to say that all is well in the land of HEA's, and I was finally able to sleep after a rather gut-wretching, nerve-wracking, nail-biting reading experience...*yay*.. just the type of book I needed to read!<br><br>I don't think the author could have written a more despicable, cold, and hateful character. Alex Markov was so wrapped up in his head, and the abuse he endured as a child,<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/whipped.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411924i/809755._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo whipped.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>that he neglected to realize the beauty (and treasure) he had right in front of him. Daisy's love had cracked, and healed his closed-off, icy heart, and it scared the hell out of him.<br><br><br>.. and Daisy, oh sweet, loving, trusting Daisy. Everyone in your life has always underestimated your strength, courage, intelligence, gentleness, and kindness. You gave all of yourself to Alex, even though the situation you were in was only a 'circumstance', you were so patient with him.. and then when you gave him your soft spot, that precious part of your heart you've never shown anyone else in your life. Alex didn't even look at it, but did the unforgiveable, He trampled it as if it was worth nothing.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/loveitneverhappenslikeyouthinkitshould.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411924ra/809756.gif" alt=" photo loveitneverhappenslikeyouthinkitshould.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When Alex finally realized that he loves you, and what he's done to you Daisy, it's too late. <br>He's already destroyed you. You've shut down, and become numb in order to protect what little of 'yourself' you have left. At this point in the book I'm so angry with Alex for not 'clueing-the-fuck-in', that I have trouble wanting to finishing the story. <br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics/hidinginsweater.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411924i/809757.jpg" alt=" photo hidinginsweater.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%204/whyareboyssuchjerks.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411924ra/809758.gif" alt=" photo whyareboyssuchjerks.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But, alas. Good things come to those who wait!<br><br>In the end, Alex's 'final act' to prove how much he loves Daisy is wonderful, and beautiful. He does the unthinkable and sacrifices his pride ... even if it means getting on his knees to beg.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pictures%203/forgiveness.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411925ra/809759.gif" alt=" photo forgiveness.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>... and it is SO worth it to read this story!<br><br><a href="http://s1095.beta.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics/review%20pics%202/theend.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411925ra/809760.gif" alt=" photo theend.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10494894150896969345" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5159702225940866955">EDIT: 27/05/14<br/><br/> 2 STARS<br/><br/>This is a difficult review to write because there wasn't anything necessarily wrong with this book, it just didn't wow me like other CR. The circus background was different and nice for a change, the story of finding love in the least likely of places and discovering your life was always meant for bigger things was sweet too. <br/><br/>I liked Alex, and not just because he was an asshole. Let me clarify: I don't like assholes by default. The typical jerk-type assholes who are dicks j</span>
  <span id="freeText5159702225940866955" style="display:none">EDIT: 27/05/14<br /><br /> 2 STARS<br /><br />This is a difficult review to write because there wasn't anything necessarily wrong with this book, it just didn't wow me like other CR. The circus background was different and nice for a change, the story of finding love in the least likely of places and discovering your life was always meant for bigger things was sweet too. <br /><br />I liked Alex, and not just because he was an asshole. Let me clarify: I don't like assholes by default. The typical jerk-type assholes who are dicks just cause', don't attract me. But men who resort to being assholes in order to cover up their vulnerabilities or insecurities? LOVE THOSE. Because they're not truly born assholes, just conditioned to be that way...have I lost you? ;-)) well at least in fiction anyway.<br /><br />Anywho, Alex was the type of ass I loved. Daisy was sweet and I didn't find any fault with her aside from being too naive at times. So really, the problem for me was lack of passion. I've read SEP before and I'm always left feeling the same way: UNSATISFIED. <br />Nothing specific, maybe not enough emotional angst, maybe not enough connection with the characters...regardless, this book as well as many others by this author are well received, so this is probably a case of, IT'S ME, NOT YOU. So i kinda liked it, but it was more just ok, it's a little forgettable for me right now. But who knows, maybe after some time I'll fondly look back on this book. Probably not.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5159702225940866955" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12045532-kiss-an-angel">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=4-and-a-half-stars">4-and-a-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=library-loan">library-loan</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1319772400" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10800193525474978144"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Susan Elizabeth Phillips is rapidly becoming one of my go-to authors. More and more these days I’m finding that contemporary romances and erotica have characters or plots so similar they become one big blur. What a treat it is to read Ms. Phillips’ older books. Some of them, such as <i>Kiss an Angel</i>, were written nearly two decades ago. Not only do they stand the test of time, they give the new kids on the block a run for their money. Every story and each character is so distinctly differe</span>
  <span id="freeText10800193525474978144" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>Susan Elizabeth Phillips is rapidly becoming one of my go-to authors. More and more these days I’m finding that contemporary romances and erotica have characters or plots so similar they become one big blur. What a treat it is to read Ms. Phillips’ older books. Some of them, such as <i>Kiss an Angel</i>, were written nearly two decades ago. Not only do they stand the test of time, they give the new kids on the block a run for their money. Every story and each character is so distinctly different. I can honestly say I’ve never read a book that combined an arranged marriage with life under the big top until now.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I, Theodosia… take thee Alexander… to be my awful wedded husband.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>I knew from the start that I would love this unique gem. Daisy is the daughter of a former ambassador to the Soviet Union and a glamorous British fashion model. Her parents never married. She was raised by her mother in an unorthodox manner but has always lived a life of privilege. She is refined but lighthearted, honest, giving, entertaining, and pure. She has a romanticized view of marriage.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436387291i/15452246.jpg" alt=" photo Daisy2_zps1v2bwzhs.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Daisy has always fallen short of her father’s expectations. After her mother’s death, Daisy gets herself into a financial mess and is facing time in jail. Her father is ready to wipe his hands of her but agrees to bail her out under certain conditions. She must marry a man of his choosing. If she stays married for six months she will receive a trust fund; if not, she will go to jail. She meets her new husband three days later. <br><br>Daisy knows nothing about Alex Markov other than he is of Russian descent. He is tall, dark and devastatingly handsome but he is brooding, humorless, intimidating, mysterious, and cold. He believes he has lost his capacity to love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436387291i/15452247._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Alex3_zpsk6jpadav.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Immediately after the wedding Alex whisks Daisy off to their new home – a run down traveling circus that he manages.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436388104i/15452317._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo CircusPoster1_zpstuhwg3bb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m not going to lie. The first part of the story is a bit of a downer as Daisy struggles to adjust to her new circumstances and she becomes a social outcast. It’s like when you can’t protect your child or best friend from the bullies at school. I pretty much hated all the characters. I’m looking at you, Sheba.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436387291i/15452250.jpg" alt=" photo Sheba1_zpscpzl767s.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kudos to Susan Elizabeth Phillips though for evoking such strong feelings in me. Then Daisy sweeps in with her ray of sunshine and you just know it’s only going to be a matter of time before her light changes everyone for good.<br><br>I loved learning about circus life. I felt like I was right in the center ring witnessing the performances and walking the fairgrounds. The smells and sights are practically tangible.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436387291i/15452251.jpg" alt=" photo peanuts_zpsqxkztgmu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ms. Phillips amazed me with how she takes the circus animals and transforms them into such key characters. I adored Sinjun, the Siberian tiger, and baby elephant Tater stole my heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436387291i/15452252._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Tater_zpsvnltexvw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Kiss an Angel</i> is a great example of the type of love story I find most gratifying: the slow burn. As the Alex and Daisy get to know each other their attraction builds gradually, and the declarations of love are slow to come. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I can’t resist you,” he said quietly. “You know that, don’t you? And I’m tired of pretending I can. But I don’t love you, Daisy, and you can’t begin to know how sorry I am about that because if I could choose anyone in this world to love, it’d be you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Their relationship is realistic and when they finally get together the payoff is great. The connection between Daisy and Alex is more than electric. It’s hot without being trashy. It’s sensual and passionate. <br><br>Susan Elizabeth Phillips tends to create strong heroines who are more than surface deep. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>His fists clenched at his sides. “Damn it! Where’s your pride?”<br><br>“Pride? It’s in my heart, of course.”<br><br>“You’re letting me demean you!”<br><br>She smiled. “You can’t do that. I can only demean myself.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Daisy is a lovely contradiction between who she truly is and how she’s viewed. She’s intelligent but considered an airhead. She’s gorgeous but having grown up in her mother’s shadow she doesn’t appreciate the strength of her own beauty. She’s a woman of principle and yet her integrity is always in question. Despite being raised by a promiscuous parent Daisy believes sex is sacred. She’s delightful in every way.<br><br>And, okay, I predicted the plot in places but that didn’t detract from my enjoyment of the journey along the way. If you’re looking for a whimsical and heartwarming story I highly recommend this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10800193525474978144" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gEWjpGIQcl4P2ju7PuiSVJH6OeZ82jSwZKH2VIpf/qOqXDkEBXifSpZoL8McHlnzon2ik4L4AvMJtM0FfwQOoA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer12061287653965821859">SUSAN ELIZABETH PHILLIPS<br/><br/>Susan Elizabeth Phillips is the creator of the sports romance, beginning with her 1989 bestseller, FANCY PANTS. An internationally acclaimed author, her books have been published in over 30 languages. She’s the only four-time recipient of the Romance Writers of America’s prestigious Favorite Book of the Year Award, and a recipient of their Lifetime Achievement Award. <br/><br/>Susan'</span>
  <span id="freeText12061287653965821859" style="display:none">SUSAN ELIZABETH PHILLIPS<br /><br />Susan Elizabeth Phillips is the creator of the sports romance, beginning with her 1989 bestseller, FANCY PANTS. An internationally acclaimed author, her books have been published in over 30 languages. She’s the only four-time recipient of the Romance Writers of America’s prestigious Favorite Book of the Year Award, and a recipient of their Lifetime Achievement Award. <br /><br />Susan's newest book, DANCE AWAY WITH ME, was published in hardcover, ebook and audiobook in June 2020. She is also the highly acclaimed author of both the CHICAGO STARS football series and the Wynette, Texas books. <br /><br />In addition to being a New York Times, Publisher’s Weekly, and USA Today bestseller, she is a hiker, lazy gardener, horrible singer, passable cook, passionate reader, wife, mother of two grown sons, and grandmother. <br /><br />You can visit Susan on Facebook, Twitter, Instagram or on her website.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SusanElizabethPhillipsNovels">https://www.facebook.com/SusanElizabe...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/sepauthor">https://twitter.com/sepauthor</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/SEPauthor/">https://www.instagram.com/SEPauthor/</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://susanelizabethphillips.com/">http://susanelizabethphillips.com/</a><br /><br /></span>
